It supports documents up to 512K tokens across 29 languages and offers 20% higher accuracy compared to its predecessor.</div></div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"row justify-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-10 col-xl-9 q-pb-xl\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--square no-border-radius q-card--flat no-shadow overflow-hidden full-width card-details relative-position bg-transparent\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-none hoverOnImage fit\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-img q-img--menu\" role=\"img\"><div style=\"padding-bottom: 52.5%;\"></div><div class=\"q-img**container absolute-full\"><img class=\"q-img**image q-img**image--with-transition q-img**image--loaded\" loading=\"lazy\" fetchpriority=\"auto\" aria-hidden=\"true\" draggable=\"false\" src=\"/assets/animation-readerlm-v2-BZGhT4e1.gif\" style=\"object-fit: cover; object-position: 50% 50%;\"></div><div class=\"q-img**content absolute-full q-anchor--skip\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"absolute-full hoverOnImage1 flex flex-center\" style=\"background: none;\"><a data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square read-more-btn\" tabindex=\"0\" href=\"/news/readerlm-v2-frontier-small-language-model-for-html-to-markdown-and-json\" style=\"font-size: 20px; padding: 24px; min-width: 0px; min-height: 0px;\"><span class=\"q-focus-helper\"></span><span class=\"q-btn**content text-center col items-center q-anchor--skip justify-center row\"><span class=\"block\">Read Release Note</span><i class=\"q-icon on-right notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"img\">arrow_forward</i></span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-pa-xl\" id=\"what_reader\"><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"what_reader\"><h2 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h2 text-weight-medium\" href=\"#what_reader\" style=\"text-decoration: none !important;\">What is Reader?</a></h2></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-img q-img--menu\" role=\"img\"><div style=\"padding-bottom: 42.5023%;\"></div><div class=\"q-img**container absolute-full\"><img class=\"q-img**image q-img**image--with-transition q-img**image--loaded\" loading=\"lazy\" fetchpriority=\"auto\" aria-hidden=\"true\" draggable=\"false\" src=\"/assets/explain-EQrFe5k3.svg\" style=\"object-fit: cover; object-position: 50% 50%;\"></div><div class=\"q-img**content absolute-full q-anchor--skip\"></div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8 col-lg-6 text-subtitle1 q-pa-lg-xl q-my-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\">Feeding web information into LLMs is an important step of grounding, yet it can be challenging. The simplest method is to scrape the webpage and feed the raw HTML. However, scraping can be complex and often blocked, and raw HTML is cluttered with extraneous elements like markups and scripts. The Reader API addresses these issues by extracting the core content from a URL and converting it into clean, LLM-friendly text, ensuring high-quality input for your agent and RAG systems.</div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\" id=\"demo1\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--bordered q-card--square no-border-radius q-card--flat no-shadow col-12 col-md-10\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert col\"><label It allows you to feed your LLM with the content behind the search results engine page. material-symbols-sharp\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">info</i> Please note that unlike the demo shown above, in practice you do not search the original question on the web for grounding. What people often do is rewrite the original question or use multi-hop questions. They read the retrieved results and then generate additional queries to gather more information as needed before arriving at a final answer.</div></div></div><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"read-image\"><h2 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h2 text-weight-medium\" href=\"#read-image\" style=\"text-decoration: none !important;\">Reader also reads images!</a></h2></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-img q-img--menu\" role=\"img\"><div style=\"padding-bottom: 56.2493%;\"></div><div class=\"q-img**container absolute-full\"><img class=\"q-img**image q-img**image--with-transition q-img**image--current\" loading=\"lazy\" fetchpriority=\"auto\" aria-hidden=\"true\" draggable=\"false\" src=\"/assets/explain2-BYDhf_rF.svg\" style=\"object-fit: cover; object-position: 50% 50%;\"></div><div class=\"q-img**loading absolute-full flex flex-center\"><svg class=\"q-spinner q-spinner-mat\" width=\"1em\" height=\"1em\" viewBox=\"25 25 50 50\"><circle class=\"path\" cx=\"50\" cy=\"50\" r=\"20\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"5\" stroke-miterlimit=\"10\"></circle></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8 col-lg-6 text-subtitle1 q-pa-lg-xl q-my-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\">Images on the webpage are automatically captioned using a vision language model in the reader and formatted as image alt tags in the output. This gives your downstream LLM just enough hints to incorporate those images into its reasoning and summarizing processes. This means you can ask questions about the images, select specific ones, or even forward their URLs to a more powerful VLM for deeper analysis!</div></div><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"read-pdf\"><h2 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h2 text-weight-medium\" href=\"#read-pdf\" style=\"text-decoration: none !important;\">Reader also reads PDFs!</a></h2></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"row q-py-xl justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-img q-img--menu\" role=\"img\"><div style=\"padding-bottom: 56.2493%;\"></div><div class=\"q-img**container absolute-full\"><img class=\"q-img**image q-img**image--with-transition q-img**image--current\" loading=\"lazy\" fetchpriority=\"auto\" aria-hidden=\"true\" draggable=\"false\" src=\"/assets/explain4-CPLfQrjf.png\" style=\"object-fit: cover; object-position: 50% 50%;\"></div><div class=\"q-img**loading absolute-full flex flex-center\"><svg class=\"q-spinner q-spinner-mat\" width=\"1em\" height=\"1em\" viewBox=\"25 25 50 50\"><circle class=\"path\" cx=\"50\" cy=\"50\" r=\"20\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"5\" stroke-miterlimit=\"10\"></circle></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8 col-lg-6 text-subtitle1 q-pa-lg-xl q-my-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\"><span data-v-5b3debb0=\"\">Yes, Reader natively supports PDF reading. It's compatible with most PDFs, including those with many images, and it's lightning fast! Combined with an LLM, you can easily build a ChatPDF or document analysis AI in no time.</span></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-btn-group row no-wrap q-btn-group--outline q-btn-group--flat q-btn-group--square inline\"><a data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square\" tabindex=\"0\" href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/55583main_vision_space_exploration2.pdf\" target=\"\_blank\" style=\"font-size: 14px; It's free!</a></h2><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"full-width text-dim text-subtitle1\"><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"row justify-center\"><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-sm-8 col-md-6\">Reader API is available for free and offers flexible rate limit and pricing. Built on a scalable infrastructure, it offers high accessibility, concurrency, and reliability. We strive to be your preferred grounding solution for your LLMs.</div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\" id=\"rate-limit\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8 text-subtitle1 q-my-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow column no-wrap full-height\"><div class=\"q-table**container q-table--horizontal-separator column no-wrap q-table**card q-table**card--dark q-dark q-table--square q-table--flat q-table--dark q-table--no-wrap my-sticky-column-table\"><div class=\"q-table**top relative-position row items-center\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark full-width q-pa-lg\" role=\"listitem\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label text-weight-bold\">Rate Limit</div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\"><span>Rate limits are tracked in three ways: <b>RPM</b> (requests per minute), and <b>TPM</b> (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.</span></div></div><div class=\"q-space\"></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center\"><label class=\"q-field row no-wrap items-start q-field--outlined q-input q-field--square q-field--dense q-field--dark\" class=\"q-field**control-container col relative-position row no-wrap q-anchor--skip\"><input class=\"q-field**native q-placeholder\" tabindex=\"0\" placeholder=\"Search\" id=\"f_3515721c-bd66-4ab1-a9e8-c3903b609c11\" type=\"text\" value=\"\"></div></div></div></label></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center\"><label class=\"q-field Find out more about the rate limits for each product and tier below.</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-focusable relative-position cursor-pointer\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp q-expansion-item**toggle-icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">keyboard_arrow_down</i></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_28209a71-b5f0-44ca-9b29-042e1307d000\" style=\"display: none;\"><div data-v-816f3729=\"\" class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow column no-wrap full-height\"><div class=\"q-table**container q-table--horizontal-separator column no-wrap q-table**card q-table**card--dark q-dark q-table--square q-table--flat q-table--dark q-table--no-wrap my-sticky-column-table\"><div class=\"q-table**top relative-position row items-center\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark full-width q-pa-lg\" role=\"listitem\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label text-weight-bold\">Rate Limit</div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\"><span>Rate limits are tracked in three ways: <b>RPM</b> (requests per minute), and <b>TPM</b> (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\">Reader captions all images at the specified URL and adds `Image [idx]: [caption]` as an alt tag (if they initially lack one). This enables downstream LLMs to interact with the images in reasoning, summarizing etc.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\" role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"f_ee2ad33d-81da-4fd2-ada9-2c4e4f3b9780\" aria-label=\"Expand &quot;What is the scalability of the Reader? Can I use it in production?</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-focusable relative-position cursor-pointer\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp q-expansion-item**toggle-icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">keyboard_arrow_down</i></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_ee2ad33d-81da-4fd2-ada9-2c4e4f3b9780\" style=\"display: none;\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\">The Reader API is designed to be highly scalable. It is auto-scaled based on the real-time traffic and the maximum concurrency requests is now around 4000. We are maintaining it actively as one of the core products of Jina AI. So feel free to use it in production.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\" role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"f_ce06482e-c48c-4c96-96c0-90ba82d61d83\" aria-label=\"Expand &quot;What is the rate limit of the Reader API?&quot;\"><div class=\"q-focus-helper\" tabindex=\"-1\"></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-item**section--avatar\"><i class=\"q-icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\"><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">What is the rate limit of the Reader API?</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-focusable relative-position cursor-pointer\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp q-expansion-item**toggle-icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">keyboard_arrow_down</i></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_ce06482e-c48c-4c96-96c0-90ba82d61d83\" style=\"display: none;\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\">Please find the latest rate limit information in the table below. Note that we are actively working on improving the rate limit and performance of the Reader API, the table will be updated accordingly.</div><a class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square\" tabindex=\"0\" href=\"#rate-limit\" style=\"padding: 24px; min-width: 0px; min-height: 0px;\"><span class=\"q-focus-helper\"></span><span class=\"q-btn**content text-center col items-center q-anchor--skip justify-center row\"><i class=\"q-icon on-left notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"img\">speed</i><span class=\"block\">Rate limit</span></span></a></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\" role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"f_f7fbd625-dd2a-43f4-8556-5177cbcf861c\" aria-label=\"Expand &quot;What is Reader-LM? How can I use it?&quot;\"><div class=\"q-focus-helper\" tabindex=\"-1\"></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-item**section--avatar\"><i class=\"q-icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\"><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">What is Reader-LM? How can I use it?</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-focusable relative-position cursor-pointer\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp q-expansion-item**toggle-icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">keyboard_arrow_down</i></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_f7fbd625-dd2a-43f4-8556-5177cbcf861c\" style=\"display: none;\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\">Reader-LM is a novel small language model (SLM) designed for data extraction and cleaning from the open web. It converts raw, noisy HTML into clean markdown, drawing inspiration from Jina Reader. With a focus on cost-efficiency and small model size, Reader-LM is both practical and powerful. It is currently available on AWS, Azure, and GCP marketplaces. If you have specific requirements, please contact us at sales AT jina.ai.</div><a class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square\" tabindex=\"0\" href=\"https://aws.amazon.com/marketplace/seller-profile?id=seller-stch2ludm6vgy\" target=\"\_blank\" style=\"padding: 24px; height: auto;\"><source data-v-d48289bf=\"\" src=\"https://jina-ai-gmbh.ghost.io/content/media/2024/10/jina-ai-rate-limit.mp4\" type=\"video/mp4\"> video_not_supported</video></div></div><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"rate-limit\"><h3 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h3 text-weight-medium\" href=\"#rate-limit\" style=\"text-decoration: none !important;\">What's the rate limit?</a></h3></div><div data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"row justify-center\"><div data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow column no-wrap full-height col-11 col-sm-9 col-md-8 col-lg-7 col-xl-6\"><div class=\"q-table**container q-table--horizontal-separator column no-wrap q-table**card q-table**card--dark q-dark q-table--square q-table--flat q-table--dark q-table--no-wrap my-sticky-column-table\"><div class=\"q-table**top relative-position row items-center\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark full-width q-pa-lg\" role=\"listitem\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label text-weight-bold\">Rate Limit</div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\"><span>Rate limits are tracked in three ways: <b>RPM</b> (requests per minute), and <b>TPM</b> (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.</span></div></div><div class=\"q-space\"></div><div class=\"q-item**section column After logging into your account on <a class=\"text-primary\" href=\"https://jina.ai/api-dashboard\">the API Key Management dashboard</a>, use the settings of the key you want to transfer out to move all remaining paid tokens.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\" role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"f_3afa4db3-5560-48d3-a68b-e852a49a9873\" aria-label=\"Expand &quot;Can I revoke my API key?&quot;\"><div class=\"q-focus-helper\" tabindex=\"-1\"></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-item**section--avatar\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">code</i></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Can I revoke my API key?</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-focusable relative-position cursor-pointer\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp q-expansion-item**toggle-icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">keyboard_arrow_down</i></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_3afa4db3-5560-48d3-a68b-e852a49a9873\" style=\"display: none;\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\">Yes, you can revoke your API key if you believe it has been compromised. Revoking a key will immediately disable it for all users who have stored it, and all remaining balance and associated properties will be permanently unusable. If the key is a premium key, you have the option to transfer the remaining paid balance to another key before revocation. Notice that this action cannot be undone. To revoke a key, go to the key settings in <a class=\"text-primary\" href=\"https://jina.ai/api-dashboard\">the API Key Management dashboard</a>.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\" role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"f_f601fdf7-3e26-4af0-ad6d-14cdbc18f51f\" aria-label=\"Expand &quot;Why is the first request for some models slow?&quot;\"><div class=\"q-focus-helper\" tabindex=\"-1\"></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-item**section--avatar\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">code</i></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Why is the first request for some models slow?</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-focusable relative-position cursor-pointer\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp q-expansion-item**toggle-icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">keyboard_arrow_down</i></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_f601fdf7-3e26-4af0-ad6d-14cdbc18f51f\" style=\"display: none;\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\">This is because our serverless architecture offloads certain models during periods of low usage. The initial request activates or 'warms up' the model, which may take a few seconds. After this initial activation, subsequent requests process much more quickly.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\" role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"f_b070f067-09af-41f5-bacb-825494423937\" aria-label=\"Expand &quot;Is user input data used for training your models?&quot;\"><div class=\"q-focus-helper\" tabindex=\"-1\"></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-item**section--avatar\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">code</i></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Is user input data used for training your models?</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-focusable relative-position cursor-pointer\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp q-expansion-item**toggle-icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\" role=\"presentation\">keyboard_arrow_down</i></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_b070f067-09af-41f5-bacb-825494423937\" style=\"display: none;\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\" style=\"white-space: pre-line;\">We adhere to a strict privacy policy and do not use user input data for training our models. This affects the quality, speed, completeness, accessibility of the content.</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center\"><label class=\"q-field row no-wrap items-start q-field--filled q-select q-field--auto-height q-select--without-input q-select--without-chips q-select--single q-field--square q-field--float q-field--dark\"><div class=\"q-field**inner relative-position col self-stretch\"><div class=\"q-field**control relative-position row no-wrap\"><div class=\"q-field**control-container col relative-position row no-wrap q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"q-field**native row items-center\"><span>Default</span></div></div></div></div></label></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Content Format </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">You can control the level of detail in the response to prevent over-filtering. The default pipeline is optimized for most websites and LLM input.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">JSON Response </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">The response will be in JSON format, containing the URL, title, content, and timestamp (if available). In Search mode, it returns a list of five entries, each following the described JSON structure.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Timeout </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Maximum page load wait time, use this if you find default browser engine is too slow on simple webpage.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Token Budget </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Limits the maximum number of tokens used for this request. Exceeding this limit will cause the request to fail.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Use ReaderLM-v2 <div class=\"q-chip row inline no-wrap items-center q-chip--outline q-chip--square q-chip--dark q-dark text-warning\"><div class=\"q-chip**content col row no-wrap items-center q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"ellipsis\">Experimental</div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Uses ReaderLM-v2 for HTML to Markdown conversion, to deliver high-quality results for websites with complex structures and contents. Costs 3x tokens!</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">A \"Buttons &amp; Links\" section will be created at the end. This helps the downstream LLMs or web agents navigating the page or take further actions.</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center\"><label class=\"q-field row no-wrap items-start q-field--filled q-select q-field--auto-height q-select--without-input q-select--without-chips q-select--single q-field--square q-field--float q-field--dark\"><div class=\"q-field**inner relative-position col self-stretch\"><div class=\"q-field**control relative-position row no-wrap\"><div class=\"q-field**control-container col relative-position row no-wrap q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"q-field**native row items-center\"><span>None</span></div></div></div></div></label></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Gather All Images At the End </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">An \"Images\" section will be created at the end. This gives the downstream LLMs an overview of all visuals on the page, which may improve reasoning.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Viewport Config <div class=\"q-chip row inline no-wrap items-center q-chip--square q-chip--dark q-dark bg-mixed-300\"><div class=\"q-chip**content col row no-wrap items-center q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"ellipsis\">POST</div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Sets browser viewport dimensions for responsive rendering.</div></div></label><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark\"><label class=\"q-field row no-wrap items-start q-field--filled q-textarea q-field--square q-field--float q-field--dark q-field--disabled full-width\"></label></div></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Forward Cookie </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Our API server can forward your custom cookie settings when accessing the URL, which is useful for pages requiring extra authentication. Note that requests with cookies will not be cached.</div></div></label><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><label class=\"q-field row no-wrap items-start q-field--filled q-select q-field--auto-height q-select--with-input q-select--with-chips q-select--multiple q-field--square q-field--float q-field--dark\"><div class=\"q-field**inner relative-position col self-stretch\"><div class=\"q-field**control relative-position row no-wrap\"><div class=\"q-field**control-container col relative-position row no-wrap q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"q-field**native row items-center\"><div class=\"q-chip row inline no-wrap items-center text-primary q-chip--colored q-chip--dense q-chip--square q-chip--dark q-dark bg-mixed-300\"><div class=\"q-chip**content col row no-wrap items-center q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"ellipsis\">&lt;cookie-name&gt;=&lt;cookie-value&gt; </div></div></div><div class=\"q-chip row inline no-wrap items-center text-primary q-chip--colored q-chip--dense q-chip--square q-chip--dark q-dark bg-mixed-300\"><div class=\"q-chip**content col row no-wrap items-center q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"ellipsis\">&lt;cookie-name-1&gt;=&lt;cookie-value&gt;; domain=&lt;cookie-1-domain&gt; </div></div></div></div></div></div></div></label></div></div></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Image Caption </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Captions all images at the specified URL, adding 'Image [idx]: [caption]' as an alt tag for those without one. This allows downstream LLMs to interact with the images in activities such as reasoning and summarizing.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Use a Proxy Server </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Our API server can utilize your proxy to access URLs, which is helpful for pages accessible only through specific proxies.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Use a Country-Specific Proxy Server </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Set country code for location-based proxy server. Use 'auto' for optimal selection or 'none' to disable.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Bypass Cached Content </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Our API caches URL contents for a certain amount of time. Set it to true to ignore the cached result and fetch the content from the URL directly.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Do Not Cache &amp; Track! </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">When enabled, the requested URL won't be cached and tracked on our server.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Github Flavored Markdown </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Opt in/out features from GFM (Github Flavored Markdown).</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center\"><label class=\"q-field row no-wrap items-start q-field--filled q-select q-field--auto-height q-select--without-input q-select--without-chips q-select--single q-field--square q-field--float q-field--dark\"><div class=\"q-field**inner relative-position col self-stretch\"><div class=\"q-field**control relative-position row no-wrap\"><div class=\"q-field**control-container col relative-position row no-wrap q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"q-field**native row items-center\"><span>Enabled</span></div></div></div></div></label></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Stream Mode </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Stream mode is beneficial for large target pages, allowing more time for the page to fully render. If standard mode results in incomplete content, consider using Stream mode.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Customize Browser Locale </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Control the browser locale to render the page. Lots of websites serve different content based on the locale.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Strictly comply robots policy </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Define bot User-Agent to check against robots.txt before fetching content.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">iframe Extraction </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Processes content from all embedded iframes in the DOM tree.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Shadow DOM Extraction </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Extracts content from all Shadow DOM roots in the document.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Follow Redirect </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Choose whether to resolve to the final destination URL after following all redirects. Enable to follow the full redirect chain.</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Local PDF/HTML file </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Use Reader on your local PDF and HTML file by uploading them. Only support pdf and html files. For HTML, please also specify a reference URL for better parsing related CSS/JS scripts.</div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center\"><label class=\"q-field row no-wrap items-start q-field--filled q-file q-field--auto-height q-field--square q-field--dark\"><div class=\"q-field**inner relative-position col self-stretch\"><div class=\"q-field**control relative-position row no-wrap\"><div class=\"q-field**prepend q-field**marginal row no-wrap items-center\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\">upload</i></div></div></div></label></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Pre-run JavaScript </div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\">Executes preprocessing JS code (inline string or remote URL).</div></div></label></div><div><label class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link Store it securely!</div></div></div></div></label></div></div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-pa-xl\" id=\"readerlm_v2_release\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"row q-mt-xl q-py-xl justify-center\"><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center col-10 col-md-8\"><h2 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h2 text-weight-medium\">ReaderLM v2: Small Language Model for HTML to Markdown and JSON</a></h2><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"full-width text-dim text-subtitle1\"><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"row justify-center\"><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-sm-8 col-md-6\">ReaderLM-v2 is a 1.5B parameter language model specialized in HTML-to-Markdown conversion and HTML-to-JSON extraction. It supports documents up to 512K tokens across 29 languages and offers 20% higher accuracy compared to its predecessor.</div></div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"row justify-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-10 col-xl-9 q-pb-xl\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--square no-border-radius q-card--flat no-shadow overflow-hidden full-width card-details relative-position bg-transparent\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-none hoverOnImage fit\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-img q-img--menu\"><div></div><div class=\"q-img**content absolute-full q-anchor--skip\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"absolute-full hoverOnImage1 flex flex-center\"><a data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square read-more-btn\"><span class=\"q-btn**content text-center col items-center q-anchor--skip justify-center row\"><span class=\"block\">Read Release Note</span><i class=\"q-icon on-right notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\">arrow_forward</i></span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-pa-xl\" id=\"what_reader\"><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"what_reader\"><h2 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h2 text-weight-medium\">What is Reader?</a></h2></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8\"></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8 col-lg-6 text-subtitle1 q-pa-lg-xl q-my-lg\">Feeding web information into LLMs is an important step of grounding, yet it can be challenging. The simplest method is to scrape the webpage and feed the raw HTML. However, scraping can be complex and often blocked, and raw HTML is cluttered with extraneous elements like markups and scripts. The Reader API addresses these issues by extracting the core content from a URL and converting it into clean, LLM-friendly text, ensuring high-quality input for your agent and RAG systems.</div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\" id=\"demo1\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--bordered q-card--square no-border-radius q-card--flat no-shadow col-12 col-md-10\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert col\"><label self-stretch\"><div class=\"q-field**control relative-position row no-wrap\"><div class=\"q-field**prepend q-field**marginal row no-wrap items-center\"><button class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable relative-position row no-wrap q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"q-field**label no-pointer-events absolute ellipsis\">Enter your URL</div></div><div class=\"q-field**append q-field**marginal row no-wrap API</div></div></div></label></div></div><button class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--flat q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square no-pointer-events absolute ellipsis\">Pose a Question</div></div><div class=\"q-field**append q-field**marginal row no-wrap items-center\"><button class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-field**bottom--animated\"><div class=\"q-field**messages col\"><div>Input a question and combine it with the fetched content for LLM to generate an answer</div></div></div></div></label></div></div></div><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"search\"><h2 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h2 text-weight-medium\">Reader for web search and SERP</a></h2></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8 col-lg-6 text-subtitle1 q-pa-lg-xl q-my-lg\"><span data-v-5b3debb0=\"\">Reader can be used as SERP API. It allows you to feed your LLM with the content behind the search results engine page. Simply prepend <code>https://s.jina.ai/?q=</code> to your query, and Reader will search the web and return the top five results with their URLs and contents, each in clean, LLM-friendly text. This way, you can always keep your LLM up-to-date, improve its factuality, and reduce hallucinations.</span></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\" id=\"demo2\"><div data-v-083190c8=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--bordered q-card--square no-border-radius q-card--flat no-shadow col-12 col-md-10\"><div data-v-083190c8=\"\" class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert\"><div data-v-083190c8=\"\" class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert col\"><label data-v-083190c8=\"\" class=\"q-field row no-wrap items-start q-field--standard q-input q-field--float q-field--labeled q-field--dark q-field--with-bottom\"><div class=\"q-field**inner relative-position col self-stretch\"><div class=\"q-field**control relative-position row no-wrap\"><div class=\"q-field**control-container col relative-position row no-wrap q-anchor--skip\"><div class=\"q-field**label no-pointer-events absolute ellipsis\">Enter your query</div></div></div><div class=\"q-field**bottom row items-start q-field**bottom--animated\"><div class=\"q-field**messages col\"><div>Type a question that requires latest information or world knowledge.</div></div></div></div></label></div><div data-v-083190c8=\"\" class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert col\"><label data-v-083190c8=\"\" class=\"q-field row no-wrap items-start q-field--standard q-input q-field--float q-field--labeled q-field--dark q-field--with-bottom q-field--readonly\"><div class=\"q-field**inner relative-position col self-stretch\"><div class=\"q-field**bottom row items-start q-field**bottom--animated\"><div class=\"q-field**messages col\">If you use this URL in code, dont forget to encode the URL.</div></div></div></label></div></div><button data-v-083190c8=\"\" class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--standard q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square full-width\" type=\"button\"><span class=\"q-btn**content text-center col items-center q-anchor--skip justify-center row\"><i class=\"q-icon on-left notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\">contact_support</i><span class=\"block\">Ask LLM w/o &amp; w/ Search Grounding</span></span></button><div data-v-083190c8=\"\" class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert text-dim\"><i data-v-083190c8=\"\" class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\">info</i> Please note that unlike the demo shown above, in practice you do not search the original question on the web for grounding. What people often do is rewrite the original question or use multi-hop questions. They read the retrieved results and then generate additional queries to gather more information as needed before arriving at a final answer.</div></div></div><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"read-image\"><h2 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h2 text-weight-medium\">Reader also reads images!</a></h2></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8 col-lg-6 text-subtitle1 q-pa-lg-xl q-my-lg\">Images on the webpage are automatically captioned using a vision language model in the reader and formatted as image alt tags in the output. This gives your downstream LLM just enough hints to incorporate those images into its reasoning and summarizing processes. This means you can ask questions about the images, select specific ones, or even forward their URLs to a more powerful VLM for deeper analysis!</div></div><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"read-pdf\"><h2 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h2 text-weight-medium\">Reader also reads PDFs!</a></h2></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"row q-py-xl justify-center items-center\"></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8 col-lg-6 text-subtitle1 q-pa-lg-xl q-my-lg\"><span data-v-5b3debb0=\"\">Yes, Reader natively supports PDF reading. It's compatible with most PDFs, including those with many images, and it's lightning fast! Combined with an LLM, you can easily build a ChatPDF or document analysis AI in no time.</span></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-btn-group row no-wrap q-btn-group--outline q-btn-group--flat q-btn-group--square inline\"><a data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square\"><span class=\"q-btn**content text-center col items-center q-anchor--skip justify-center row\"><span class=\"block\">Original PDF</span></span></a><a data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square\"><span class=\"q-btn**content text-center col items-center q-anchor--skip justify-center row\"><span class=\"block\">Reader Result</span></span></a></div></div><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\"><h2 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h2 text-weight-medium\">The best part? It's free!</a></h2><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"full-width text-dim text-subtitle1\"><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"row justify-center\"><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-sm-8 col-md-6\">Reader API is available for free and offers flexible rate limit and pricing. Built on a scalable infrastructure, it offers high accessibility, concurrency, and reliability. We strive to be your preferred grounding solution for your LLMs.</div></div></div></div><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-my-xl row justify-center items-center\" id=\"rate-limit\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-md-8 text-subtitle1 q-my-lg\"><div data-v-5b3debb0=\"\" class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow column no-wrap full-height\"><div class=\"q-table**container q-table--horizontal-separator column no-wrap q-table**card q-table**card--dark q-dark q-table--square q-table--flat q-table--dark q-table--no-wrap my-sticky-column-table\"><div class=\"q-table**top relative-position row items-center\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark full-width q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label text-weight-bold\">Rate Limit</div><div class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--caption text-caption\"><span>Rate limits are tracked in three ways: <b>RPM</b> (requests per minute), and <b>TPM</b> (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.</span></div></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side should I use the Reader API instead of scraping the page myself?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_999e4171-9c6a-426d-9a13-de91d9d29353\"><div particularly with complex or dynamic pages. The Reader API provides a streamlined, reliable output of clean, LLM-ready text.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Does the Reader API support multiple languages?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_aa7c845f-d9d1-434a-920d-ec12364deb55\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">The Reader API returns content in the original language of the URL. It does not provide translation services.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">How does image caption work in Reader?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_bc237efb-00b7-45c2-ac6f-7691b8b44820\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">Reader captions all images at the specified URL and adds `Image [idx]: [caption]` as an alt tag (if they initially lack one). This enables downstream LLMs to interact with the images in reasoning, summarizing etc.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">What is the scalability of the Reader? Can I use it in production?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_ee2ad33d-81da-4fd2-ada9-2c4e4f3b9780\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">The Reader API is designed to be highly scalable. It is auto-scaled based on the real-time traffic and the maximum concurrency requests is now around 4000. We are maintaining it actively as one of the core products of Jina AI. So feel free to use it in production.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">What is the rate limit of the Reader API?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_ce06482e-c48c-4c96-96c0-90ba82d61d83\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">Please find the latest rate limit information in the table below. Note that we are actively working on improving the rate limit and performance of the Reader API, the table will be updated accordingly.</div><a class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square\"><span class=\"q-btn**content text-center col items-center q-anchor--skip justify-center row\"><span class=\"block\">Rate limit</span></span></a></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">What is Reader-LM? How can I use it?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_f7fbd625-dd2a-43f4-8556-5177cbcf861c\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">Reader-LM is a novel small language model (SLM) designed for data extraction and cleaning from the open web. It converts raw, noisy HTML into clean markdown, drawing inspiration from Jina Reader. With a focus on cost-efficiency and small model size, Reader-LM is both practical and powerful. It is currently available on AWS, Azure, and GCP marketplaces. If you have specific requirements, please contact us at sales AT jina.ai.</div><a class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"get-api-key\"><h3 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" class=\"text-white my-h3 text-weight-medium\">How to get my API key?</a></h3></div><div data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"row justify-center\"><div data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"col-11 col-sm-9 col-md-8 col-lg-7 col-xl-6\"></div></div><div data-v-46d92e03=\"\" data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"q-py-xl column text-center items-center\" id=\"rate-limit\"><h3 data-v-46d92e03=\"\"><a data-v-46d92e03=\"\" q-card--flat no-shadow column no-wrap full-height col-11 col-sm-9 col-md-8 col-lg-7 col-xl-6\"></div></div><div data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"row justify-center\"><div data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"q-list q-list--dark q-list--padding col-11 col-sm-9 col-md-8 col-lg-7 col-xl-6\"><div data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"q-py-md\"></div><div data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--header\">API-related common questions</div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-item**section--avatar\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\">code</i></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Can I use the same API key for reader, embedding, reranking, classifying and fine-tuning APIs?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_f1540307-b463-4bef-8651-2c0313977ee4\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">Yes, the same API key is valid for all search foundation products from Jina AI. This includes the reader, embedding, reranking, classifying and fine-tuning APIs, with tokens shared between the all services.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Can I monitor the token usage of my API key?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_a5ed254f-8194-4dec-9a69-30c926cac4cf\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">Yes, token usage can be monitored in the 'API Key &amp; Billing' tab by entering your API key, allowing you to view the recent usage history and remaining tokens. If you have logged in to the API dashboard, these details can also be viewed in the 'Manage API Key' tab.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">What should I do if I forget my API key?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_d8657048-a61b-4146-98de-7a4c811703af\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">If you have misplaced a topped-up key and wish to retrieve it, please contact support AT jina.ai with your registered email for assistance. It's recommended to log in to keep your API key securely stored and easily accessible.</div><a class=\"q-btn q-btn-item non-selectable no-outline q-btn--outline q-btn--rectangle q-btn--square q-btn--actionable q-focusable q-hoverable q-btn--square\"><span class=\"q-btn**content text-center col items-center q-anchor--skip justify-center row\"><span class=\"block\">Contact</span></span></a></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Do API keys expire?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_8b3b4ea7-d008-4a23-8524-96e0fcd43b4e\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">No, our API keys do not have an expiration date. However, if you suspect your key has been compromised and wish to retire it, please contact our support team for assistance. You can also revoke your key in <a class=\"text-primary\">the API Key Management dashboard</a>.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Can I transfer tokens between API keys?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_60b96fc6-a256-4aeb-b8e4-859363cc9607\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">Yes, you can transfer tokens from a premium key to another. After logging into your account on </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Can I revoke my API key?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_3afa4db3-5560-48d3-a68b-e852a49a9873\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">Yes, you can revoke your API key if you believe it has been compromised. Revoking a key will immediately disable it for all users who have stored it, and all remaining balance and associated properties will be permanently unusable. If the key is a premium key, you have the option to transfer the remaining paid balance to another key before revocation. Notice that this action cannot be undone. To revoke a key, go to the key settings in </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Why is the first request for some models slow?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_f601fdf7-3e26-4af0-ad6d-14cdbc18f51f\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">This is because our serverless architecture offloads certain models during periods of low usage. The initial request activates or 'warms up' the model, which may take a few seconds. After this initial activation, subsequent requests process much more quickly.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Is user input data used for training your models?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_b070f067-09af-41f5-bacb-825494423937\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">We adhere to a strict privacy policy and do not use user input data for training our models. We are also SOC 2 Type I and Type II compliant, ensuring high standards of security and privacy.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div data-v-d48289bf=\"\" class=\"q-item**label q-item**label--header\">Billing-related common questions</div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--side justify-center q-item**section--avatar\"><i class=\"q-icon notranslate material-symbols material-symbols-sharp\">attach_money</i></div><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Is billing based on the number of sentences or requests?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_3eb6fce9-ef29-43d2-b4d3-70d7608b1551\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">Our pricing model is based on the total number of tokens processed, allowing users the flexibility to allocate these tokens across any number of sentences, offering a cost-effective solution for diverse text analysis requirements.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item q-item-type q-expansion-item--collapsed q-expansion-item--standard bg-dark\"><div class=\"q-expansion-item**container relative-position\"><div class=\"q-item q-item-type row no-wrap q-item--dark q-item--clickable q-link cursor-pointer q-focusable q-hoverable\"><div class=\"q-item**section column q-item**section--main justify-center\"><div class=\"q-item**label\">Is there a free trial available for new users?</div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item**content relative-position\" id=\"f_67c55c43-55d8-449a-ba83-48376edefcf3\"><div class=\"q-card q-card--dark q-dark q-card--flat no-shadow bg-mixed-200\"><div class=\"q-card**section q-card**section--vert q-pa-lg\"><div class=\"q-py-lg\">We offer a welcoming free trial to new users, which includes ten millions tokens for use with any of our models, facilitated by an auto-generated API key. Once the free token limit is reached, users can easily purchase additional tokens for their API keys via the 'Buy tokens' tab.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"q-expansion-item <button><span><i>sync</i></span></button>\n</div>\n</div></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>This is your unique key. Store it securely!</div></div></div>\n</div></label></div>\n</div></div></div>\n</div>\n<div>\n<div><div>\n<h2><a>ReaderLM v2: Small Language Model for HTML to Markdown and JSON</a></h2>\n<div><div><div>ReaderLM-v2 is a 1.5B parameter language model specialized in HTML-to-Markdown conversion and HTML-to-JSON extraction. It supports documents up to 512K tokens across 29 languages and offers 20% higher accuracy compared to its predecessor.</div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div><div><div><div>\n<div><img src=\"/assets/animation-readerlm-v2-BZGhT4e1.gif\"></div>\n<div><div><a href=\"/news/readerlm-v2-frontier-small-language-model-for-html-to-markdown-and-json\"><span><span>Read Release Note</span><i>arrow_forward</i></span></a></div></div>\n</div></div></div></div></div>\n</div>\n<div>\n<div><h2><a href=\"#what_reader\">What is Reader?</a></h2></div>\n<div><div><div><div><img src=\"/assets/explain-EQrFe5k3.svg\"></div></div></div></div>\n<div><div>Feeding web information into LLMs is an important step of grounding, yet it can be challenging. The simplest method is to scrape the webpage and feed the raw HTML. However, scraping can be complex and often blocked, and raw HTML is cluttered with extraneous elements like markups and scripts. The Reader API addresses these issues by extracting the core content from a URL and converting it into clean, LLM-friendly text, ensuring high-quality input for your agent and RAG systems.</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><label><div>\n<div>\n<div><button><span><i>casino</i></span></button></div>\n<div>\n<input><div>Enter your URL</div>\n</div>\n<div><button><span><i>open_in_new</i></span></button></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>Click below to fetch the source code of the page directly</div></div></div>\n</div></label></div>\n<hr>\n<div><label><div>\n<div>\n<div>\n<input><div>Reader URL</div>\n</div>\n<div>\n<button><span><i>content_copy</i></span></button><button><span><i>open_in_new</i></span></button>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div><div>Click below to obtain the content through our Reader API</div></div>\n</div></label></div>\n</div>\n<hr>\n<button><span><i>download</i><span>Fetch Content</span></span></button><hr>\n<div>\n<div>\n<span>Raw HTML</span><div><button><span><i>content_copy</i></span></button></div>\n</div>\n<hr>\n<div>\n<span>Reader Output</span><div><button><span><i>content_copy</i></span></button></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<hr>\n<div><label><div>\n<div>\n<div>\n<input><div>Pose a Question</div>\n</div>\n<div><button><span><i>send</i></span></button></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>Input a question and combine it with the fetched content for LLM to generate an answer</div></div></div>\n</div></label></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><h2><a href=\"#search\">Reader for web search and SERP</a></h2></div>\n<div><div><div><div><img src=\"/assets/explain3-CqNg2V0h.svg\"></div></div></div></div>\n<div><div><span>Reader can be used as SERP API. It allows you to feed your LLM with the content behind the search results engine page. Simply prepend <code>https://s.jina.ai/?q=</code> to your query, and Reader will search the web and return the top five results with their URLs and contents, each in clean, LLM-friendly text. This way, you can always keep your LLM up-to-date, improve its factuality, and reduce hallucinations.</span></div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><label><div>\n<div>\n<div><button><span><i>casino</i></span></button></div>\n<div>\n<input><div>Enter your query</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>Type a question that requires latest information or world knowledge.</div></div></div>\n</div></label></div>\n<hr>\n<div><label><div>\n<div>\n<div>\n<input><div>Reader URL</div>\n</div>\n<div>\n<button><span><i>content_copy</i></span></button><button><span><i>open_in_new</i></span></button>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div><div>If you use this URL in code, dont forget to encode the URL.</div></div>\n</div></label></div>\n</div>\n<hr>\n<button><span><i>contact_support</i><span>Ask LLM w/o &amp; w/ Search Grounding</span></span></button><hr>\n<div>\n<i>info</i> Please note that unlike the demo shown above, in practice you do not search the original question on the web for grounding. What people often do is rewrite the original question or use multi-hop questions. They read the retrieved results and then generate additional queries to gather more information as needed before arriving at a final answer.</div>\n</div></div>\n<div><h2><a href=\"#read-image\">Reader also reads images!</a></h2></div>\n<div><div><div><div><img src=\"/assets/explain2-BYDhf_rF.svg\"></div></div></div></div>\n<div><div>Images on the webpage are automatically captioned using a vision language model in the reader and formatted as image alt tags in the output. This gives your downstream LLM just enough hints to incorporate those images into its reasoning and summarizing processes. This means you can ask questions about the images, select specific ones, or even forward their URLs to a more powerful VLM for deeper analysis!</div></div>\n<div><h2><a href=\"#read-pdf\">Reader also reads PDFs!</a></h2></div>\n<div><div><div><div><img src=\"/assets/explain4-CPLfQrjf.png\"></div></div></div></div>\n<div><div><span>Yes, Reader natively supports PDF reading. It's compatible with most PDFs, including those with many images, and it's lightning fast! Combined with an LLM, you can easily build a ChatPDF or document analysis AI in no time.</span></div></div>\n<div><div>\n<a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/55583main_vision_space_exploration2.pdf\"><span><i>open_in_new</i><span>Original PDF</span></span></a><hr>\n<a href=\"https://r.jina.ai/https://www.nasa.gov/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/55583main_vision_space_exploration2.pdf\"><span><i>open_in_new</i><span>Reader Result</span></span></a>\n</div></div>\n<div>\n<h2><a>The best part? It's free!</a></h2>\n<div><div><div>Reader API is available for free and offers flexible rate limit and pricing. Built on a scalable infrastructure, it offers high accessibility, concurrency, and reliability. We strive to be your preferred grounding solution for your LLMs.</div></div></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div>Rate Limit</div>\n<div><span>Rate limits are tracked in three ways: <b>RPM</b> (requests per minute), and <b>TPM</b> (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.</span></div>\n</div>\n<div><label><div><div><div><input></div></div></div></label></div>\n<div><label><div><div>\n<div><div>\n<span>Columns</span><input>\n</div></div>\n<div><i>arrow_drop_down</i></div>\n</div></div></label></div>\n<div><button><span><i>fullscreen</i></span></button></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><table>\n<thead><tr>\n<th></th>\n<th>Product</th>\n<th>API
