top-up on low token balance</div>\n<div>Recommended for uninterrupted service in production. When your token balance drops below the set threshold, we will automatically recharge your saved payment method for the last purchased package, until the threshold is met.</div>\n<div>\n<i>info</i> We introduced a new pricing model on May 6th, 2025. If you enabled auto-recharge before this date, you'll continue to pay the old price (the one when you purchased). The new pricing only applies if you modify your auto-recharge settings or purchase a new API key.</div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div><i>check</i></div></div></div></div>\n<div><label><div><div>\n<div>\n<div><span>&lt; 1M Tokens</span></div>\n<div>Top up when</div>\n</div>\n<div><i>arrow_drop_down</i></div>\n</div></div></label></div></label>\n</div></div>\n</div></div></div></div>\n</div>\n<div>\n<div><h2><a href=\"#faq\">FAQ</a></h2></div>\n<div><div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>What are the costs associated with using the Reader API?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>The Reader API is free of charge and does not require an API key. Simply prepend 'https://r.jina.ai/' to your URL.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>How does the Reader API function?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>The Reader API uses a proxy to fetch any URL, rendering its content in a browser to extract high-quality main content.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>Is the Reader API open source?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Yes, the Reader API is open source and available on the Jina AI GitHub repository.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>What is the typical latency for the Reader API?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>The Reader API generally processes URLs and returns content within 2 seconds, although complex or dynamic pages might require more time.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>Why should I use the Reader API instead of scraping the page myself?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Scraping can be complicated and unreliable, particularly with complex or dynamic pages. The Reader API provides a streamlined, reliable output of clean, LLM-ready text.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>Does the Reader API support multiple languages?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>The Reader API returns content in the original language of the URL. It does not provide translation services.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>What should I do if a website blocks the Reader API?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>If you experience blocking issues, please contact our support team for assistance and resolution.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>Can the Reader API extract content from PDF files?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Yes, the Reader API can natively extract content from PDF files.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>Can the Reader API process media content from web pages?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Currently, the Reader API does not process media content, but future enhancements will include image captioning and video summarization.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>Is it possible to use the Reader API on local HTML files?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>No, the Reader API can only process content from publicly accessible URLs.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>Does Reader API cache the content?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>If you request the same URL within 5 minutes, the Reader API will return the cached content.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>Can I use the Reader API to access content behind a login?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Unfortunately not.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>Can I use the Reader API to access PDF on arXiv?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Yes, you can either use the native PDF support from the Reader (https://r.jina.ai/https://arxiv.org/pdf/2310.19923v4) or use the HTML version from the arXiv (https://r.jina.ai/https://arxiv.org/html/2310.19923v4)</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>How does image caption work in Reader?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Reader captions all images at the specified URL and adds `Image [idx]: [caption]` as an alt tag (if they initially lack one). This enables downstream LLMs to interact with the images in reasoning, summarizing etc.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>What is the scalability of the Reader? Can I use it in production?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>The Reader API is designed to be highly scalable. It is auto-scaled based on the real-time traffic and the maximum concurrency requests is now around 4000. We are maintaining it actively as one of the core products of Jina AI. So feel free to use it in production.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>What is the rate limit of the Reader API?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>Please find the latest rate limit information in the table below. Note that we are actively working on improving the rate limit and performance of the Reader API, the table will be updated accordingly.</div>\n<a href=\"#rate-limit\"><span><i>speed</i><span>Rate limit</span></span></a>\n</div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i><img src=\"/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg\"></i></div>\n<div><div>What is Reader-LM? How can I use it?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>Reader-LM is a novel small language model (SLM) designed for data extraction and cleaning from the open web. It converts raw, noisy HTML into clean markdown, drawing inspiration from Jina Reader. With a focus on cost-efficiency and small model size, Reader-LM is both practical and powerful. It is currently available on AWS, Azure, and GCP marketplaces. If you have specific requirements, please contact us at sales AT jina.ai.</div>\n<a href=\"https://aws.amazon.com/marketplace/seller-profile?id=seller-stch2ludm6vgy\"><span><i>launch</i><span>AWS SageMaker</span></span></a><a href=\"https://console.cloud.google.com/marketplace/browse?q=jina&amp;pli=1&amp;inv=1&amp;invt=AbmydQ\"><span><i>launch</i><span>Google Cloud</span></span></a><a href=\"https://azuremarketplace.microsoft.com/en-US/marketplace/apps?page=1&amp;search=jina\"><span><i>launch</i><span>Microsoft Azure</span></span></a>\n</div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><h3><a href=\"#get-api-key\">How to get my API key?</a></h3></div>\n<div><div><video><source src=\"https://jina-ai-gmbh.ghost.io/content/media/2024/10/jina-ai-rate-limit.mp4\"> video_not_supported</source></video></div></div>\n<div><h3><a href=\"#rate-limit\">What's the rate limit?</a></h3></div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div>Rate Limit</div>\n<div><span>Rate limits are tracked in three ways: <b>RPM</b> (requests per minute), and <b>TPM</b> (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.</span></div>\n</div>\n<div><label><div><div><div><input></div></div></div></label></div>\n<div><label><div><div>\n<div><div>\n<span>Columns</span><input>\n</div></div>\n<div><i>arrow_drop_down</i></div>\n</div></div></label></div>\n<div><button><span><i>fullscreen</i></span></button></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><table>\n<thead><tr>\n<th></th>\n<th>Product</th>\n<th>API questions</div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>code</i></div>\n<div><div>Can I use the same API key for reader, embedding, reranking, classifying and fine-tuning APIs?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Yes, the same API key is valid for all search foundation products from Jina AI. This includes the reader, embedding, reranking, classifying and fine-tuning APIs, with tokens shared between the all services.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>code</i></div>\n<div><div>Can I monitor the token usage of my API key?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Yes, token usage can be monitored in the 'API Key &amp; Billing' tab by entering your API key, allowing you to view the recent usage history and remaining tokens. If you have logged in to the API dashboard, these details can also be viewed in the 'Manage API Key' tab.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>code</i></div>\n<div><div>What should I do if I forget my API key?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>If you have misplaced a topped-up key and wish to retrieve it, please contact support AT jina.ai with your registered email for assistance. It's recommended to log in to keep your API key securely stored and easily accessible.</div>\n<a href=\"/contact-sales\"><span><span>Contact</span></span></a>\n</div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>code</i></div>\n<div><div>Do API keys expire?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>No, our API keys do not have an expiration date. However, if you suspect your key has been compromised and wish to retire it, please contact our support team for assistance. You can also revoke your key in <a href=\"https://jina.ai/api-dashboard\">the API Key Management dashboard</a>.</div>\n<a href=\"/contact-sales\"><span><span>Contact</span></span></a>\n</div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>code</i></div>\n<div><div>Can I transfer tokens between API keys?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Yes, you can transfer tokens from a premium key to another. After logging into your account on <a href=\"https://jina.ai/api-dashboard\">the API Key Management dashboard</a>, use the settings of the key you want to transfer out to move all remaining paid tokens.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>code</i></div>\n<div><div>Can I revoke my API key?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Yes, you can revoke your API key if you believe it has been compromised. Revoking a key will immediately disable it for all users who have stored it, and all remaining balance and associated properties will be permanently unusable. If the key is a premium key, you have the option to transfer the remaining paid balance to another key before revocation. Notice that this action cannot be undone. To revoke a key, go to the key settings in <a href=\"https://jina.ai/api-dashboard\">the API Key Management dashboard</a>.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>code</i></div>\n<div><div>Why is the first request for some models slow?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>This is because our serverless architecture offloads certain models during periods of low usage. The initial request activates or 'warms up' the model, which may take a few seconds. After this initial activation, subsequent requests process much more quickly.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>code</i></div>\n<div><div>Is user input data used for training your models?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>We adhere to a strict privacy policy and do not use user input data for training our models. We are also SOC 2 Type I and Type II compliant, ensuring high standards of security and privacy.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div>Billing-related common questions</div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>attach_money</i></div>\n<div><div>Is billing based on the number of sentences or requests?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Our pricing model is based on the total number of tokens processed, allowing users the flexibility to allocate these tokens across any number of sentences, offering a cost-effective solution for diverse text analysis requirements.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>attach_money</i></div>\n<div><div>Is there a free trial available for new users?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>We offer a welcoming free trial to new users, which includes ten millions tokens for use with any of our models, facilitated by an auto-generated API key. Once the free token limit is reached, users can easily purchase additional tokens for their API keys via the 'Buy tokens' tab.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>attach_money</i></div>\n<div><div>Are tokens charged for failed requests?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>No, tokens are not deducted for failed requests.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>attach_money</i></div>\n<div><div>What payment methods are accepted?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Payments are processed through Stripe, supporting a variety of payment methods including credit cards, Google Pay, and PayPal for your convenience.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n<div><div>\n<div>\n<div><i>attach_money</i></div>\n<div><div>Is invoicing available for token purchases?</div></div>\n<div><i>keyboard_arrow_down</i></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div><div>Yes, an invoice will be issued to the email address associated with your Stripe account upon the purchase of tokens.</div></div></div></div>\n</div></div>\n</div></div>\n</div></main></div>\n<div>\n<div>\n<div><div>\n<div>Offices</div>\n<div>\n<div><i>location_on</i></div>\n<div>\n<div>Sunnyvale, the web and get SERP\n_ \* _\nParameters\n*arrow_drop_down*\nThe target URL to fetch content from\nAdd API Key for Higher Rate Limit \nEnter your Jina API key to access a higher rate limit. For latest rate limit information, please refer to the table below.\n[*open_in_new* Learn more](https://jina.ai/reader#rate-limit)\nBrowser Engine (Quality/Speed) \nChoose the browser engine for fetching the webpage content. This affects the quality, speed, completeness, accessibility of the content.\nDefault\n*arrow_drop_down*\nContent Format \nYou can control the level of detail in the response to prevent over-filtering. The default pipeline is optimized for most websites and LLM input.\nDefault\n*arrow_drop_down*\nJSON Response \nThe response will be in JSON format, containing the URL, title, content, and timestamp (if available). In Search mode, it returns a list of five entries, each following the described JSON structure.\nTimeout \nMaximum page load wait time, use this if you find default browser engine is too slow on simple webpage.\nToken Budget \nLimits the maximum number of tokens used for this request. Exceeding this limit will cause the request to fail.\nUse ReaderLM-v2 \nExperimental\nUses ReaderLM-v2 for HTML to Markdown conversion, to deliver high-quality results for websites with complex structures and contents. Costs 3x tokens!\n[*open_in_new* Learn more](https://jina.ai/news/readerlm-v2-frontier-small-language-model-for-html-to-markdown-and-json)\nCSS Selector: Only \nList of CSS selectors to target specific page elements.\nbody \n.class \n#id \nCSS Selector: Wait-For \nCSS selectors to wait for before returning results.\nbody \n.class \n#id \nCSS Selector: Excluding \nCSS selectors for elements to remove (headers, footers, etc.).\nheader \n.class \n#id \nRemove All Images \nRemove all images from the response.\nGather All Links At the End \nA \"Buttons & Links\" section will be created at the end. This helps the downstream LLMs or web agents navigating the page or take further actions.\nNone\n*arrow_drop_down*\nGather All Images At the End \nAn \"Images\" section will be created at the end. This gives the downstream LLMs an overview of all visuals on the page, which may improve reasoning.\nNone\n*arrow_drop_down*\nViewport Config \nPOST\nSets browser viewport dimensions for responsive rendering.\n[*open_in_new* Learn more](https://pptr.dev/api/puppeteer.viewport)\nForward Cookie \nOur API server can forward your custom cookie settings when accessing the URL, which is useful for pages requiring extra authentication. Note that requests with cookies will not be cached.\n[*open_in_new* Learn more](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Headers/Set-Cookie)\n<cookie-name>=<cookie-value>\n<cookie-name-1>=<cookie-value>; domain=<cookie-1-domain>\nImage Caption \nCaptions all images at the specified URL, adding 'Image [idx]: [caption]' as an alt tag for those without one. This allows downstream LLMs to interact with the images in activities such as reasoning and summarizing.\nUse a Proxy Server \nOur API server can utilize your proxy to access URLs, which is helpful for pages accessible only through specific proxies.\n[*open_in_new* Learn more](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proxy_server)\nUse a Country-Specific Proxy Server \nSet country code for location-based proxy server. Use 'auto' for optimal selection or 'none' to disable.\nBypass Cached Content \nOur API caches URL contents for a certain amount of time. Set it to true to ignore the cached result and fetch the content from the URL directly.\nDo Not Cache & Track! \nWhen enabled, the requested URL won't be cached and tracked on our server.\nGithub Flavored Markdown \nOpt in/out features from GFM (Github Flavored Markdown).\nEnabled\n*arrow_drop_down*\nStream Mode \nStream mode is beneficial for large target pages, allowing more time for the page to fully render. If standard mode results in incomplete content, consider using Stream mode.\n[*open_in_new* Learn more](https://github.com/jina-ai/reader?tab=readme-ov-file#streaming-mode)\nCustomize Browser Locale \nControl the browser locale to render the page. Lots of websites serve different content based on the locale.\n[*open_in_new* Learn more](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Navigator/language)\nStrictly comply robots policy \nDefine bot User-Agent to check against robots.txt before fetching content.\niframe Extraction \nProcesses content from all embedded iframes in the DOM tree.\nShadow DOM Extraction \nExtracts content from all Shadow DOM roots in the document.\nFollow Redirect \nChoose whether to resolve to the final destination URL after following all redirects. Enable to follow the full redirect chain.\nLocal PDF/HTML file \nPOST\nUse Reader on your local PDF and HTML file by uploading them. Only support pdf and html files. For HTML, please also specify a reference URL for better parsing related CSS/JS scripts.\n*upload*\nPre-run JavaScript \nPOST\nExecutes preprocessing JS code (inline string or remote URL).\n[*open_in_new* Learn more](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript)\nHeading Style \nSets markdown heading format (passed to Turndown).\nAlternative Heading Syntax\n*arrow_drop_down*\nHorizontal Rule Style \nDefines markdown horizontal rule format (passed to Turndown).\nBullet Point Style \nSets bullet list marker character (passed to Turndown).\n_\n*arrow_drop_down*\nEmphasis Style \nDefines markdown emphasis delimiter (passed to Turndown).\n*\n_arrow_drop_down*\nStrong Emphasis Style \nSets markdown strong emphasis delimiter (passed to Turndown).\n**\n*arrow_drop_down*\nLink Style \nDetermines markdown link format (passed to Turndown).\nInline\n*arrow_drop_down*\nEU Compliance \nExperimental\nAll infrastructure and data processing operations reside entirely within EU jurisdiction.\n\* \* _\n*upload*\nRequest\nGET\nBash\nLanguage\n*arrow_drop_down*\n*wrap_text*\n`\ncurl \"https://r.jina.ai/https://example.com\"\n\n`\n\n*content_copy*\n_ \* _\n*send* GET RESPONSE\n_ \* _\n*key*\nAPI key\n*visibility_off* *content_copy*\n_ \* _\nAvailable tokens\n0 *sync*\nThis is your unique key. Store it securely!\n## ReaderLM v2: Small Language Model for HTML to Markdown and JSON\nReaderLM-v2 is a 1.5B parameter language model specialized in HTML-to-Markdown conversion and HTML-to-JSON extraction. It supports documents up to 512K tokens across 29 languages and offers 20% higher accuracy compared to its predecessor.\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/animation-readerlm-v2-BZGhT4e1.gif)\n[Read Release Note *arrow_forward*](https://jina.ai/news/readerlm-v2-frontier-small-language-model-for-html-to-markdown-and-json)\n## [What is Reader?](https://jina.ai/reader/#what_reader)\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/explain-EQrFe5k3.svg)\nFeeding web information into LLMs is an important step of grounding, yet it can be challenging. The simplest method is to scrape the webpage and feed the raw HTML. However, scraping can be complex and often blocked, and raw HTML is cluttered with extraneous elements like markups and scripts. The Reader API addresses these issues by extracting the core content from a URL and converting it into clean, LLM-friendly text, ensuring high-quality input for your agent and RAG systems.\n*casino*\nEnter your URL\n*open_in_new*\nClick below to fetch the source code of the page directly\n_ \* _\nReader URL\n*content_copy* *open_in_new*\nClick below to obtain the content through our Reader API\n_ \* _\n*download* Fetch Content\n_ \* _\nRaw HTML\n *content_copy*\n_ \* _\nReader Output\n *content_copy*\n_ \* _\nPose a Question\n*send*\nInput a question and combine it with the fetched content for LLM to generate an answer\n## [Reader for web search and SERP](https://jina.ai/reader/#search)\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/explain3-CqNg2V0h.svg)\nReader can be used as SERP API. It allows you to feed your LLM with the content behind the search results engine page. Simply prepend `https://s.jina.ai/?q=` to your query, and Reader will search the web and return the top five results with their URLs and contents, each in clean, LLM-friendly text. This way, you can always keep your LLM up-to-date, improve its factuality, and reduce hallucinations.\n*casino*\nEnter your query\nType a question that requires latest information or world knowledge.\n_ \* _\nReader URL\n*content_copy* *open_in_new*\nIf you use this URL in code, dont forget to encode the URL.\n_ \* _\n*contact_support* Ask LLM w/o & w/ Search Grounding\n_ \* _\n*info* Please note that unlike the demo shown above, in practice you do not search the original question on the web for grounding. What people often do is rewrite the original question or use multi-hop questions. They read the retrieved results and then generate additional queries to gather more information as needed before arriving at a final answer.\n## [Reader also reads images!](https://jina.ai/reader/#read-image)\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/explain2-BYDhf_rF.svg)\nImages on the webpage are automatically captioned using a vision language model in the reader and formatted as image alt tags in the output. This gives your downstream LLM just enough hints to incorporate those images into its reasoning and summarizing processes. This means you can ask questions about the images, select specific ones, or even forward their URLs to a more powerful VLM for deeper analysis!\n## [Reader also reads PDFs!](https://jina.ai/reader/#read-pdf)\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/explain4-CPLfQrjf.png)\nYes, Reader natively supports PDF reading. It's compatible with most PDFs, including those with many images, and it's lightning fast! Combined with an LLM, you can easily build a ChatPDF or document analysis AI in no time.\n[*open_in_new* Original PDF](https://www.nasa.gov/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/55583main_vision_space_exploration2.pdf)\n_ \* \*\n[_open_in_new_ Reader Result](https://r.jina.ai/https://www.nasa.gov/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/55583main_vision_space_exploration2.pdf)\n## The best part? It's free!\nReader API is available for free and offers flexible rate limit and pricing. Built on a scalable infrastructure, it offers high accessibility, concurrency, and reliability. We strive to be your preferred grounding solution for your LLMs.\nRate Limit\nRate limits are tracked in three ways: **RPM** (requests per minute), and **TPM** (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.\nColumns\n*arrow_drop_down*\n*fullscreen*\n| Product | API Endpoint | Description _arrow_upward_ Find out more about the rate limits for each product and tier below.\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nRate Limit\nRate limits are tracked in three ways: **RPM** (requests per minute), and **TPM** (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When your token balance drops below the set threshold, we will automatically recharge your saved payment method for the last purchased package, until the threshold is met.\n_info* We introduced a new pricing model on May 6th, 2025. If you enabled auto-recharge before this date, you'll continue to pay the old price (the one when you purchased). The new pricing only applies if you modify your auto-recharge settings or purchase a new API key.\n*check*\n< 1M Tokens\nTop up when\n*arrow_drop_down*\n## [FAQ](https://jina.ai/reader/#faq)\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat are the costs associated with using the Reader API?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API is free of charge and does not require an API key. Simply prepend 'https://r.jina.ai/' to your URL.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nHow does the Reader API function?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API uses a proxy to fetch any URL, rendering its content in a browser to extract high-quality main content.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nIs the Reader API open source?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, the Reader API is open source and available on the Jina AI GitHub repository.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat is the typical latency for the Reader API?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API generally processes URLs and returns content within 2 seconds, although complex or dynamic pages might require more time.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhy should I use the Reader API instead of scraping the page myself?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nScraping can be complicated and unreliable, particularly with complex or dynamic pages. The Reader API provides a streamlined, reliable output of clean, LLM-ready text.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nDoes the Reader API support multiple languages?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API returns content in the original language of the URL. It does not provide translation services.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat should I do if a website blocks the Reader API?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nIf you experience blocking issues, please contact our support team for assistance and resolution.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nCan the Reader API extract content from PDF files?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, the Reader API can natively extract content from PDF files.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nCan the Reader API process media content from web pages?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nCurrently, the Reader API does not process media content, but future enhancements will include image captioning and video summarization.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nIs it possible to use the Reader API on local HTML files?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nNo, the Reader API can only process content from publicly accessible URLs.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nDoes Reader API cache the content?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nIf you request the same URL within 5 minutes, the Reader API will return the cached content.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nCan I use the Reader API to access content behind a login?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nUnfortunately not.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nCan I use the Reader API to access PDF on arXiv?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, you can either use the native PDF support from the Reader (https://r.jina.ai/https://arxiv.org/pdf/2310.19923v4) or use the HTML version from the arXiv (https://r.jina.ai/https://arxiv.org/html/2310.19923v4)\n_![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)_\nHow does image caption work in Reader?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nReader captions all images at the specified URL and adds `Image [idx]: [caption]` as an alt tag (if they initially lack one). This enables downstream LLMs to interact with the images in reasoning, summarizing etc.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat is the scalability of the Reader? Can I use it in production?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API is designed to be highly scalable. It is auto-scaled based on the real-time traffic and the maximum concurrency requests is now around 4000. We are maintaining it actively as one of the core products of Jina AI. So feel free to use it in production.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat is the rate limit of the Reader API?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nPlease find the latest rate limit information in the table below. Note that we are actively working on improving the rate limit and performance of the Reader API, the table will be updated accordingly.\n[_speed_ Rate limit](https://jina.ai/reader/#rate-limit)\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat is Reader-LM? How can I use it?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nReader-LM is a novel small language model (SLM) designed for data extraction and cleaning from the open web. It converts raw, noisy HTML into clean markdown, drawing inspiration from Jina Reader. With a focus on cost-efficiency and small model size, Reader-LM is both practical and powerful. It is currently available on AWS, Azure, and GCP marketplaces. If you have specific requirements, please contact us at sales AT jina.ai.\n[_launch_ AWS SageMaker](https://aws.amazon.com/marketplace/seller-profile?id=seller-stch2ludm6vgy)[ _launch_ Google Cloud](https://console.cloud.google.com/marketplace/browse?q=jina&pli=1&inv=1&invt=AbmydQ)[ _launch_ Microsoft Azure](https://azuremarketplace.microsoft.com/en-US/marketplace/apps?page=1&search=jina)\n### [How to get my API key?](https://jina.ai/reader/#get-api-key)\nvideo_not_supported\n### [What's the rate limit?](https://jina.ai/reader/#rate-limit)\nRate Limit\nRate limits are tracked in three ways: **RPM** (requests per minute), and **TPM** (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.\nColumns\n*arrow_drop_down*\n*fullscreen*\n| Product | API Endpoint | Description _arrow_upward_ questions\n_code*\nCan I use the same API key for reader, embedding, reranking, classifying and fine-tuning APIs?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, the same API key is valid for all search foundation products from Jina AI. This includes the reader, embedding, reranking, classifying and fine-tuning APIs, with tokens shared between the all services.\n*code*\nCan I monitor the token usage of my API key?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, token usage can be monitored in the 'API Key & Billing' tab by entering your API key, allowing you to view the recent usage history and remaining tokens. If you have logged in to the API dashboard, these details can also be viewed in the 'Manage API Key' tab.\n*code*\nWhat should I do if I forget my API key?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nIf you have misplaced a topped-up key and wish to retrieve it, please contact support AT jina.ai with your registered email for assistance. It's recommended to log in to keep your API key securely stored and easily accessible.\n[Contact](https://jina.ai/contact-sales)\n*code*\nDo API keys expire?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nNo, our API keys do not have an expiration date. However, if you suspect your key has been compromised and wish to retire it, please contact our support team for assistance. You can also revoke your key in [the API Key Management dashboard](https://jina.ai/api-dashboard).\n[Contact](https://jina.ai/contact-sales)\n*code*\nCan I transfer tokens between API keys?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, you can transfer tokens from a premium key to another. After logging into your account on [the API Key Management dashboard](https://jina.ai/api-dashboard), use the settings of the key you want to transfer out to move all remaining paid tokens.\n*code*\nCan I revoke my API key?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, you can revoke your API key if you believe it has been compromised. Revoking a key will immediately disable it for all users who have stored it, and all remaining balance and associated properties will be permanently unusable. If the key is a premium key, you have the option to transfer the remaining paid balance to another key before revocation. Notice that this action cannot be undone. To revoke a key, go to the key settings in [the API Key Management dashboard](https://jina.ai/api-dashboard).\n*code*\nWhy is the first request for some models slow?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThis is because our serverless architecture offloads certain models during periods of low usage. The initial request activates or 'warms up' the model, which may take a few seconds. After this initial activation, subsequent requests process much more quickly.\n*code*\nIs user input data used for training your models?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nWe adhere to a strict privacy policy and do not use user input data for training our models. We are also SOC 2 Type I and Type II compliant, ensuring high standards of security and privacy.\nBilling-related common questions\n*attach_money*\nIs billing based on the number of sentences or requests?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nOur pricing model is based on the total number of tokens processed, allowing users the flexibility to allocate these tokens across any number of sentences, offering a cost-effective solution for diverse text analysis requirements.\n*attach_money*\nIs there a free trial available for new users?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nWe offer a welcoming free trial to new users, which includes ten millions tokens for use with any of our models, facilitated by an auto-generated API key. The default pipeline is optimized for most websites and LLM input.\nDefault\n*arrow_drop_down*\nJSON Response \nThe response will be in JSON format, containing the URL, title, content, and timestamp (if available). In Search mode, it returns a list of five entries, each following the described JSON structure.\nTimeout \nMaximum page load wait time, use this if you find default browser engine is too slow on simple webpage.\nToken Budget \nLimits the maximum number of tokens used for this request. Exceeding this limit will cause the request to fail.\nUse ReaderLM-v2 \nExperimental\nUses ReaderLM-v2 for HTML to Markdown conversion, to deliver high-quality results for websites with complex structures and contents. Note that requests with cookies will not be cached.\n*open_in_new* Learn more\u27e826\u27e9\n<cookie-name>=<cookie-value>\n<cookie-name-1>=<cookie-value>; domain=<cookie-1-domain>\nImage Caption \nCaptions all images at the specified URL, adding 'Image [idx]: [caption]' as an alt tag for those without one. This allows downstream LLMs to interact with the images in activities such as reasoning and summarizing.\nUse a Proxy Server \nOur API server can utilize your proxy to access URLs, which is helpful for pages accessible only through specific proxies.\n*open_in_new* Learn more\u27e827\u27e9\nUse a Country-Specific Proxy Server \nSet country code for location-based proxy server. Use 'auto' for optimal selection or 'none' to disable.\nBypass Cached Content \nOur API caches URL contents for a certain amount of time. Set it to true to ignore the cached result and fetch the content from the URL directly.\nDo Not Cache & Track! \nWhen enabled, the requested URL won't be cached and tracked on our server.\nGithub Flavored Markdown \nOpt in/out features from GFM (Github Flavored Markdown).\nEnabled\n*arrow_drop_down*\nStream Mode \nStream mode is beneficial for large target pages, allowing more time for the page to fully render. If standard mode results in incomplete content, consider using Stream mode.\n*open_in_new* Learn more\u27e828\u27e9\nCustomize Browser Locale \nControl the browser locale to render the page. Lots of websites serve different content based on the locale.\n*open_in_new* Learn more\u27e829\u27e9\nStrictly comply robots policy \nDefine bot User-Agent to check against robots.txt before fetching content.\niframe Extraction \nProcesses content from all embedded iframes in the DOM tree.\nShadow DOM Extraction \nExtracts content from all Shadow DOM roots in the document.\nFollow Redirect \nChoose whether to resolve to the final destination URL after following all redirects. Enable to follow the full redirect chain.\nLocal PDF/HTML file \nPOST\nUse Reader on your local PDF and HTML file by uploading them. Only support pdf and html files. Store it securely!\n## ReaderLM v2: Small Language Model for HTML to Markdown and JSON\nReaderLM-v2 is a 1.5B parameter language model specialized in HTML-to-Markdown conversion and HTML-to-JSON extraction. It supports documents up to 512K tokens across 29 languages and offers 20% higher accuracy compared to its predecessor.\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/animation-readerlm-v2-BZGhT4e1.gif)\nRead Release Note *arrow_forward*\u27e824\u27e9\n## What is Reader?\u27e831\u27e9\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/explain-EQrFe5k3.svg)\nFeeding web information into LLMs is an important step of grounding, yet it can be challenging. The simplest method is to scrape the webpage and feed the raw HTML. However, scraping can be complex and often blocked, and raw HTML is cluttered with extraneous elements like markups and scripts. The Reader API addresses these issues by extracting the core content from a URL and converting it into clean, LLM-friendly text, ensuring high-quality input for your agent and RAG systems.\n*casino*\nEnter your URL\n*open_in_new*\nClick below to fetch the source code of the page directly\n_ \* _\nReader URL\n*content_copy* *open_in_new*\nClick below to obtain the content through our Reader API\n_ \* _\n*download* Fetch Content\n_ \* _\nRaw HTML\n *content_copy*\n_ \* _\nReader Output\n *content_copy*\n_ \* _\nPose a Question\n*send*\nInput a question and combine it with the fetched content for LLM to generate an answer\n## Reader for web search and SERP\u27e832\u27e9\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/explain3-CqNg2V0h.svg)\nReader can be used as SERP API. It allows you to feed your LLM with the content behind the search results engine page. Simply prepend `https://s.jina.ai/?q=` to your query, and Reader will search the web and return the top five results with their URLs and contents, each in clean, LLM-friendly text. This way, you can always keep your LLM up-to-date, improve its factuality, and reduce hallucinations.\n*casino*\nEnter your query\nType a question that requires latest information or world knowledge.\n_ \* _\nReader URL\n*content_copy* *open_in_new*\nIf you use this URL in code, dont forget to encode the URL.\n_ \* _\n*contact_support* Ask LLM w/o & w/ Search Grounding\n_ \* _\n*info* Please note that unlike the demo shown above, in practice you do not search the original question on the web for grounding. What people often do is rewrite the original question or use multi-hop questions. They read the retrieved results and then generate additional queries to gather more information as needed before arriving at a final answer.\n## Reader also reads images!\u27e833\u27e9\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/explain2-BYDhf_rF.svg)\nImages on the webpage are automatically captioned using a vision language model in the reader and formatted as image alt tags in the output. This gives your downstream LLM just enough hints to incorporate those images into its reasoning and summarizing processes. This means you can ask questions about the images, select specific ones, or even forward their URLs to a more powerful VLM for deeper analysis!\n## Reader also reads PDFs!\u27e834\u27e9\n![](https://jina.ai/assets/explain4-CPLfQrjf.png)\nYes, Reader natively supports PDF reading. It's compatible with most PDFs, including those with many images, and it's lightning fast! Combined with an LLM, you can easily build a ChatPDF or document analysis AI in no time.\n*open_in_new* Original PDF\u27e835\u27e9\n_ \* _\n*open_in_new* Reader Result\u27e836\u27e9\n## The best part? It's free!\nReader API is available for free and offers flexible rate limit and pricing. Built on a scalable infrastructure, it offers high accessibility, concurrency, and reliability. We strive to be your preferred grounding solution for your LLMs.\nRate Limit\nRate limits are tracked in three ways: **RPM** (requests per minute), and **TPM** (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.\nColumns\n*arrow_drop_down*\n*fullscreen*\n| Product | API Endpoint | Description *arrow_upward* Find out more about the rate limits for each product and tier below.\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nRate Limit\nRate limits are tracked in three ways: **RPM** (requests per minute), and **TPM** (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.\nColumns\n*arrow_drop_down*\n*fullscreen*\n| Product | API Endpoint | Description _arrow_upward_ When your token balance drops below the set threshold, we will automatically recharge your saved payment method for the last purchased package, until the threshold is met.\n_info* We introduced a new pricing model on May 6th, 2025. If you enabled auto-recharge before this date, you'll continue to pay the old price (the one when you purchased). The new pricing only applies if you modify your auto-recharge settings or purchase a new API key.\n*check*\n< 1M Tokens\nTop up when\n*arrow_drop_down*\n## FAQ\u27e838\u27e9\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat are the costs associated with using the Reader API?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API is free of charge and does not require an API key. Simply prepend 'https://r.jina.ai/' to your URL.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nHow does the Reader API function?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API uses a proxy to fetch any URL, rendering its content in a browser to extract high-quality main content.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nIs the Reader API open source?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, the Reader API is open source and available on the Jina AI GitHub repository.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat is the typical latency for the Reader API?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API generally processes URLs and returns content within 2 seconds, although complex or dynamic pages might require more time.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhy should I use the Reader API instead of scraping the page myself?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nScraping can be complicated and unreliable, particularly with complex or dynamic pages. The Reader API provides a streamlined, reliable output of clean, LLM-ready text.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nDoes the Reader API support multiple languages?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API returns content in the original language of the URL. It does not provide translation services.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat should I do if a website blocks the Reader API?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nIf you experience blocking issues, please contact our support team for assistance and resolution.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nCan the Reader API extract content from PDF files?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, the Reader API can natively extract content from PDF files.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nCan the Reader API process media content from web pages?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nCurrently, the Reader API does not process media content, but future enhancements will include image captioning and video summarization.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nIs it possible to use the Reader API on local HTML files?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nNo, the Reader API can only process content from publicly accessible URLs.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nDoes Reader API cache the content?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nIf you request the same URL within 5 minutes, the Reader API will return the cached content.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nCan I use the Reader API to access content behind a login?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nUnfortunately not.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nCan I use the Reader API to access PDF on arXiv?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, you can either use the native PDF support from the Reader (https://r.jina.ai/https://arxiv.org/pdf/2310.19923v4) or use the HTML version from the arXiv (https://r.jina.ai/https://arxiv.org/html/2310.19923v4)\n_![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)_\nHow does image caption work in Reader?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nReader captions all images at the specified URL and adds `Image [idx]: [caption]` as an alt tag (if they initially lack one). This enables downstream LLMs to interact with the images in reasoning, summarizing etc.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat is the scalability of the Reader? Can I use it in production?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThe Reader API is designed to be highly scalable. It is auto-scaled based on the real-time traffic and the maximum concurrency requests is now around 4000. We are maintaining it actively as one of the core products of Jina AI. So feel free to use it in production.\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat is the rate limit of the Reader API?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nPlease find the latest rate limit information in the table below. Note that we are actively working on improving the rate limit and performance of the Reader API, the table will be updated accordingly.\n*speed* Rate limit\u27e839\u27e9\n*![](https://jina.ai/assets/reader-D06QTWF1.svg)*\nWhat is Reader-LM? How can I use it?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nReader-LM is a novel small language model (SLM) designed for data extraction and cleaning from the open web. It converts raw, noisy HTML into clean markdown, drawing inspiration from Jina Reader. With a focus on cost-efficiency and small model size, Reader-LM is both practical and powerful. It is currently available on AWS, Azure, and GCP marketplaces. If you have specific requirements, please contact us at sales AT jina.ai.\n*launch* AWS SageMaker\u27e840\u27e9 _launch_ Google Cloud\u27e841\u27e9 _launch_ Microsoft Azure\u27e842\u27e9\n### How to get my API key?\u27e843\u27e9\nvideo*not_supported\n### What's the rate limit?\u27e839\u27e9\nRate Limit\nRate limits are tracked in three ways: **RPM** (requests per minute), and **TPM** (tokens per minute). Limits are enforced per IP/API key and will be triggered when either the RPM or TPM threshold is reached first. When you provide an API key in the request header, we track rate limits by key rather than IP address.\nColumns\n_arrow_drop_down*\n*fullscreen*\n| Product | API Endpoint | Description _arrow_upward_ | Segmenter API | `https://api.jina.ai/v1/segment` | Tokenize and segment long text | 20 RPM | 200 RPM | 1,000 RPM | 0.3s | Token is not counted as usage. | GET/POST \nAPI-related common questions\n_code*\nCan I use the same API key for reader, embedding, reranking, classifying and fine-tuning APIs?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, the same API key is valid for all search foundation products from Jina AI. This includes the reader, embedding, reranking, classifying and fine-tuning APIs, with tokens shared between the all services.\n*code*\nCan I monitor the token usage of my API key?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, token usage can be monitored in the 'API Key & Billing' tab by entering your API key, allowing you to view the recent usage history and remaining tokens. If you have logged in to the API dashboard, these details can also be viewed in the 'Manage API Key' tab.\n*code*\nWhat should I do if I forget my API key?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nIf you have misplaced a topped-up key and wish to retrieve it, please contact support AT jina.ai with your registered email for assistance. It's recommended to log in to keep your API key securely stored and easily accessible.\nContact\u27e812\u27e9\n*code*\nDo API keys expire?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nNo, our API keys do not have an expiration date. However, if you suspect your key has been compromised and wish to retire it, please contact our support team for assistance. You can also revoke your key in the API Key Management dashboard\u27e844\u27e9.\nContact\u27e812\u27e9\n*code*\nCan I transfer tokens between API keys?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, you can transfer tokens from a premium key to another. After logging into your account on the API Key Management dashboard\u27e844\u27e9, use the settings of the key you want to transfer out to move all remaining paid tokens.\n*code*\nCan I revoke my API key?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, you can revoke your API key if you believe it has been compromised. Revoking a key will immediately disable it for all users who have stored it, and all remaining balance and associated properties will be permanently unusable. If the key is a premium key, you have the option to transfer the remaining paid balance to another key before revocation. Notice that this action cannot be undone. To revoke a key, go to the key settings in the API Key Management dashboard\u27e844\u27e9.\n*code*\nWhy is the first request for some models slow?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nThis is because our serverless architecture offloads certain models during periods of low usage. The initial request activates or 'warms up' the model, which may take a few seconds. After this initial activation, subsequent requests process much more quickly.\n*code*\nIs user input data used for training your models?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nWe adhere to a strict privacy policy and do not use user input data for training our models. We are also SOC 2 Type I and Type II compliant, ensuring high standards of security and privacy.\nBilling-related common questions\n*attach_money*\nIs billing based on the number of sentences or requests?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nOur pricing model is based on the total number of tokens processed, allowing users the flexibility to allocate these tokens across any number of sentences, offering a cost-effective solution for diverse text analysis requirements.\n*attach_money*\nIs there a free trial available for new users?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nWe offer a welcoming free trial to new users, which includes ten millions tokens for use with any of our models, facilitated by an auto-generated API key. Once the free token limit is reached, users can easily purchase additional tokens for their API keys via the 'Buy tokens' tab.\n*attach_money*\nAre tokens charged for failed requests?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nNo, tokens are not deducted for failed requests.\n*attach_money*\nWhat payment methods are accepted?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nPayments are processed through Stripe, supporting a variety of payment methods including credit cards, Google Pay, and PayPal for your convenience.\n*attach_money*\nIs invoicing available for token purchases?\n*keyboard_arrow_down*\nYes, an invoice will be issued to the email address associated with your Stripe account upon the purchase of tokens.\nOffices\n*location_on*\nSunnyvale, CA\n710 Lakeway Dr, Ste 200, Sunnyvale, CA 94085, USA\n*location_on*\nBerlin, Germany (HQ)\nPrinzessinnenstra\u00dfe 19-20, 10969 Berlin, Germany\n*location_on*\nBeijing, China\nLevel 5, Building 6, No.48 Haidian West St. Beijing, China\n*location_on*\nShenzhen, China\n402 Floor 4, Fu'an Technology Building, Shenzhen, China\nSearch Foundation\nReader\u27e819\u27e9Embeddings\u27e845\u27e9Reranker\u27e846\u27e9DeepSearch\u27e847\u27e9Classifier\u27e848\u27e9Segmenter\u27e849\u27e9API Documentation\u27e810\u27e9\nGet Jina API key\nRate Limit\u27e850\u27e9API Status\u27e851\u27e9\nCompany\nAbout us\u27e811\u27e9Contact sales\u27e812\u27e9Newsroom\u27e82\u27e9Intern program\u27e813\u27e9Join us _open_in_new_\u27e814\u27e9 Download logo _open_in_new_\u27e815\u27e9\nTerms\nSecurity\u27e852\u27e9Terms & Conditions\u27e853\u27e9Privacy\u27e854\u27e9Manage Cookies\u27e855\u27e9;)![\u27e856\u27e9](https://app.eu.vanta.com/jinaai/trust/vz7f4mohp0847aho84lmva)\n[](https://x.com/jinaAI_)[](https://www.linkedin.com/company/jinaai/)[](https://github.com/jina-ai)_![\u27e857\u27e9_](https://huggingface.co/jinaai)[](https://discord.jina.ai)_email_\nJina AI \u00a9 2020-2025. \n",
